<h1>2021级高二寒假数学作业1 直线与方程</h1>
<h2>单选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>A</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>C</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>A,B,D</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>A,C,D</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <i>x</i>－<i>y</i>＋2＝0 </p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    设△<i>ABC</i>的重心为<i>G</i>，垂心为<i>H</i>.由重心坐标公式得<i>x</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/74f6381bda0d46d697043abc5d4a7fb6.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/501b324c57924b899c04deb732b0592f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<i>y</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/b5ace1c48c004776bc2b8dacda209881.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/0be832eae9164a2ba8c4e27a491e1e82.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以<i>G</i>(－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/501b324c57924b899c04deb732b0592f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/0be832eae9164a2ba8c4e27a491e1e82.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>).由题知，△<i>ABC</i>的边<i>AC</i>上的高线所在直线方程为<i>x</i>＝0，直线<i>BC</i>：<i>y</i>＝<i>x</i>＋4，<i>A</i>(2，0)，所以△<i>ABC</i>的边<i>BC</i>上的高线所在直线方程为<i>y</i>＝－<i>x</i>＋2，所以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/a12883713e8c48d8a98b31fc13f310fc.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>⇒<i>H</i>(0，2)，所以欧拉线<i>GH</i>的方程为<i>x</i>－<i>y</i>＋2＝0.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    (<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/806f7044c9754c91bb2b80e43911e7c5.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/0be832eae9164a2ba8c4e27a491e1e82.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>) </p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    因为<i>PA</i>＋<i>PC</i>≥<i>AC</i>，当且仅当点<i>A</i>，<i>P</i>，<i>C</i>三点共线，且点<i>P</i>位于<i>A</i>，<i>C</i>之间时等号成立，<i>PB</i>＋<i>PD</i>≥<i>BD</i>，当且仅当<i>B</i>，<i>P</i>，<i>D</i>三点共线，且点<i>P</i>位于<i>B</i>，<i>D</i>之间时等号成立，所以<i>PA</i>＋<i>PB</i>＋<i>PC</i>＋<i>PD</i>≥<i>AC</i>＋<i>BD</i>，当且仅当<i>P</i>为直线<i>AC</i>与<i>BD</i>的交点时等号成立．因为<i>A</i>(－1，0)，<i>B</i>(1，0)，<i>C</i>(2，3)，<i>D</i>(－2，6)，所以直线<i>AC</i>的方程为<i>x</i>－<i>y</i>＋1＝0，直线<i>BD</i>的方程为2<i>x</i>＋<i>y</i>－2＝0，所以直线<i>AC</i>与<i>BD</i>的交点为(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/806f7044c9754c91bb2b80e43911e7c5.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/0be832eae9164a2ba8c4e27a491e1e82.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>)，所以当点<i>P</i>的坐标为(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/806f7044c9754c91bb2b80e43911e7c5.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/0be832eae9164a2ba8c4e27a491e1e82.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>)时，<i>PA</i>＋<i>PB</i>＋<i>PC</i>＋<i>PD</i>取最小值．
</p>
<p
    style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-align:center;text-indent:2em">
    <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/e45b4f16a6914a3c8fabe7aa1b484cb6.png?"
        style="width:135px;height:129px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
</p><br>

<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1) ∵
    <i>B</i>(－1，－2)，<i>C</i>(6，3)，直线<i>BC</i>的斜率<i>k</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/282b916f3f6d4a92bae1d0eaf9f1c08a.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/79fc13ca44b54e2ebba9692cb7152da0.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，故边<i>BC</i>上的高线所在直线的斜率<i>k</i><sub>1</sub>＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/3bd8c178013a46b3a1eb71d0f8956302.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，故边<i>BC</i>上的高线所在直线的方程为<i>y</i>－6＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/3bd8c178013a46b3a1eb71d0f8956302.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>(<i>x</i>－1)，即7<i>x</i>＋5<i>y</i>－37＝0.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    <i>BC</i>的中点<i>D</i>(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/9a0ac1b15567456ca0ba7f862c4855b0.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/b312ffa98b5a4e75a8a063fe119fdcc7.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>)，中线<i>AD</i>所在直线的斜率<i>k</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/473a1281069d420284e9730999a2539e.png?"
        style="height:66px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/4a66ce2922e24e73918046cd30541198.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，故边<i>BC</i>上的中线<i>AD</i>所在直线的方程为<i>y</i>－6＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/4a66ce2922e24e73918046cd30541198.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>(<i>x</i>－1)，即11<i>x</i>＋3<i>y</i>－29＝0.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    由已知得直线<i>l</i>斜率存在，设<i>l</i>：<i>y</i>＝<i>kx</i>－1(<i>k</i>&gt;0).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    由<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/259186d7fedd4e9388013d93987f5f8d.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>得<i>M</i>(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/b98213bea67541b2bd87034b1e337461.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，1).又0&lt;<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>&lt;1，所以<i>k</i>&gt;2.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    由<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/3ec704032a784dba9ee69785c6ba2296.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/85f90d33f5824f2eae47cd444e549b16.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/85f90d33f5824f2eae47cd444e549b16.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    <i>S</i>＝<i>S</i><sub>△OPM</sub>－<i>S</i><sub>△OPN</sub>＝<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>(<i>k</i>&gt;2).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(3)
    设<i>t</i>＝<i>k</i>－2，则<i>t</i>&gt;0，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">

<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    因为过点<i>P</i>(1，2)作直线<i>l</i>分别与<i>x</i>，<i>y</i>轴正半轴交于点<i>A</i>，<i>B</i>，且△<i>AOB</i>是等腰直角三角形，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以直线<i>l</i>的倾斜角为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/38bc7d8389d54e99ba84507a0c15ee28.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以直线<i>l</i>的斜率<i>k</i>＝tan <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/38bc7d8389d54e99ba84507a0c15ee28.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝－1，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以直线<i>l</i>的方程为<i>y</i>－2＝－(<i>x</i>－1)，即<i>x</i>＋<i>y</i>－3＝0.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    设<i>A</i>(<i>a</i>，0)，<i>B</i>(0，<i>b</i>)(<i>a</i>，<i>b</i>&gt;0)，直线<i>l</i>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/c450303bd5144bd1ac7ae118f89f3840/2a101604e53049329b9031257d7d78bc.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＋<span>​</span><img

<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    由题意可得，圆心为(2，0)，半径为2，则圆的方程为(<i>x</i>－2)<sup>2</sup>＋<i>y</i><sup>2</sup>＝4.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    由(1)可知圆<i>C</i>半径<i>r</i>＝2.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    设圆心(2，0)到<i>l</i>的距离为<i>d</i>，则<i>d</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/6a19407953d9494ba17654767852c571/13f5f7c78e8e47c19a215fadf102a0d0.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝1.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    由垂径定理得<i>AB</i>＝2<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/6a19407953d9494ba17654767852c571/6cfb5116f5264f2cb58c53c65efb0239.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝2<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/6a19407953d9494ba17654767852c571/9b14b8a758ac40f9b7146a4303504f6b.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    设圆心<i>C</i>(<i>a</i>，0)，<i>a</i>&gt;0，半径为<i>r</i>，则圆心<i>C</i>(<i>a</i>，0)到直线<i>y</i>＝<i>x</i>的距离为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/6a19407953d9494ba17654767852c571/4d54f7e726094c90967c571e46c4e266.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以8＋(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/6a19407953d9494ba17654767852c571/4d54f7e726094c90967c571e46c4e266.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>)<sup>2</sup>＝<i>r</i><sup>2</sup>且<i>a</i><sup>2</sup>＋6＝<i>r</i><sup>2</sup>，解得<i>a</i>＝2，<i>r</i><sup>2</sup>＝10，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以圆<i>C</i>的方程为(<i>x</i>－2)<sup>2</sup>＋<i>y</i><sup>2</sup>＝10.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    设<i>M</i>(<i>x</i><sub>1</sub>，<i>y</i><sub>1</sub>)，<i>N</i>(<i>x</i><sub>2</sub>，<i>y</i><sub>2</sub>)是直线<i>y</i>＝－<i>x</i>＋<i>m</i>与圆<i>C</i>的交点．
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    将<i>y</i>＝－<i>x</i>＋<i>m</i>代入圆<i>C</i>的方程，得2<i>x</i><sup>2</sup>－(4＋2<i>m</i>)<i>x</i>＋<i>m</i><sup>2</sup>－6＝0.
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <i>Δ</i>＝－4(<i>m</i><sup>2</sup>－4<i>m</i>－16)&gt;0，所以2－2<span>​</span><img

<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/01bc63696fe94236b3fd1951d298a0b2/f1478dc2df1d4e71b5ce7381f4d8bb6b.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> </p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    △<i>F</i><sub>1</sub><i>AB</i>的周长等于<i>AB</i>＋<i>AF</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>BF</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>AB</i>＋2<i>a</i>－<i>AF</i><sub>2</sub>＋2<i>a</i>－<i>BF</i><sub>2</sub>＝4<i>a</i>＋<i>AB</i>－(<i>AF</i><sub>2</sub>＋<i>BF</i><sub>2</sub>).∵
    <i>AF</i><sub>2</sub>＋<i>BF</i><sub>2</sub>≥<i>AB</i>，当且仅当<i>A</i>，<i>B</i>，<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>三点共线时等号成立，∴
    4<i>a</i>＋<i>AB</i>－(<i>AF</i><sub>2</sub>＋<i>BF</i><sub>2</sub>)≤4<i>a</i>＋<i>AB</i>－<i>AB</i>＝4<i>a</i>，即△<i>F</i><sub>1</sub><i>AB</i>的周长的最大值为4<i>a</i>＝8，得<i>a</i>＝2.由椭圆方程可得<i>b</i><sup>2</sup>＝1，则<i>c</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/01bc63696fe94236b3fd1951d298a0b2/21cf41aaa0024c17ba13b29370799aee.png?"

    所以线段<i>OT</i>长度的取值范围是(0，2).</p>

<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    设<i>F</i><sub>1</sub><i>F</i><sub>2</sub>＝2<i>c</i>，则由题意可知<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/01bc63696fe94236b3fd1951d298a0b2/9d2e953ffce64a7390c37168e4f114e9.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>⇒<i>a</i>＝2，<i>c</i>＝1⇒<i>b</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/27/01bc63696fe94236b3fd1951d298a0b2/a22ff1ad116e443b97bca03f7fd06b35.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    故椭圆<i>C</i>的方程为<span>​</span><img

<h1>2021级高二寒假数学作业5 抛物线</h1>
<h2>单选题</h2>

        alt=""><span>​</span>消去<i>y</i>得4<i>x</i><sup>2</sup>－5<i>px</i>＋<i>p</i><sup>2</sup>＝0，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>x</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>x</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/e9c16eed1eea4b07acf25190efeda88f/e610a80a3b284030b951559565527e0a.png?"

<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    因为抛物线<i>H</i>的方程为<i>y</i><sup>2</sup>＝2<i>px</i>，<i>M</i>在抛物线<i>H</i>上且横坐标为5，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>M</i>的纵坐标为±<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/e9c16eed1eea4b07acf25190efeda88f/71c12b72f27a471ea6d9e448b6bbb376.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/e9c16eed1eea4b07acf25190efeda88f/71c12b72f27a471ea6d9e448b6bbb376.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>)时，如图，过点<i>M</i>作<i>MN</i>⊥<i>OF</i>，垂足为<i>N</i>.
</p>
<p
    style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-align:center;text-indent:2em">
    <span>​</span><img

        style="width:112px;height:134px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">因为cos

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>

    ∠<i>MFN</i>＝<span>​</span><img

        alt=""><span>​</span>)时，<i>p</i>＝2，所以抛物线<i>H</i>的方程为<i>y</i><sup>2</sup>＝4<i>x</i>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    证明：设直线<i>AB</i>：<i>x</i>＝<i>my</i>＋1，<i>A</i>(<i>x</i><sub>1</sub>，<i>y</i><sub>1</sub>)，<i>B</i>(<i>x</i><sub>2</sub>，<i>y</i><sub>2</sub>)，<i>C</i>(－1，<i>n</i>).

<h2>单选题</h2>

<p><strong>02.</strong>

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.∵
    <i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>n</i>＝10或<i>n</i>＝11时，<i>f</i>(<i>n</i>)有最小值100.</p>

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，即25<i>n</i>&gt;24<i>n</i>＋18，解得<i>n</i>&gt;18，又<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>，故满足<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>&gt;<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/da077b94b3e4473b9dadc7def111c163/0c9053bce66b423686cb3050eb3bad2f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的最小正整数为19.</p>

<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em"> 解：(1)
    <i>a</i><sub>11</sub>＝<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＋(11－1)×2＝0，故<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝－20，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    故<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝－20＋(<i>n</i>－1)×2＝2<i>n</i>－22，即<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝2<i>n</i>－22.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    当1≤<i>n</i>≤10时，<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>&lt;0；当<i>n</i>＝11时，<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝0；当<i>n</i>≥12时，<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>&gt;0，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    故当<i>n</i>＝10，11时，<i>S</i><sub>n</sub>有最小值且最小值为<i>S</i><sub>10</sub>＝<i>S</i><sub>11</sub>＝－20×11＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/da077b94b3e4473b9dadc7def111c163/a3a5efa1bc264f7ba8fc161564dd2ed1.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>×2＝－110.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em"> 解：(1) ∵
    <i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝6－<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>，即<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>＝6，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;2<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＝6，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＝3.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    设等差数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}的公差为<i>d</i>(<i>d</i>≠0)，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">∵
    <i>a</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/da077b94b3e4473b9dadc7def111c163/0a0287885f004532a7cfe4532fb1d3a7.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>＝<i>a</i><sub>2</sub><i>a</i><sub>14</sub>，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;(<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＋3<i>d</i>)<sup>2</sup>＝<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>(<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＋12<i>d</i>)，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>d</i><sup>2</sup>＝2<i>d</i>，解得<i>d</i>＝0(舍)或<i>d</i>＝2，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>－<i>d</i>＝3－2＝1，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}的通项公式为</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝1＋(<i>n</i>－1)×2＝2<i>n</i>－1(<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    由(1)知，<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝2<i>n</i>－1(<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>)，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝(<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＋1)(<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＋3)＝2<i>n</i>(2<i>n</i>＋2)＝4<i>n</i>(<i>n</i>＋1).
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    假设存在正整数<i>m</i>，使得<i>b</i><sub>m</sub>＋8＝<i>b</i><sub>m＋2</sub>－<i>b</i><sub>m＋1</sub>成立，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    即4<i>m</i>(<i>m</i>＋1)＋8＝4(<i>m</i>＋2)(<i>m</i>＋3)－4(<i>m</i>＋1)(<i>m</i>＋2).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    化简整理，得<i>m</i><sup>2</sup>－<i>m</i>－2＝0，即(<i>m</i>－2)(<i>m</i>＋1)＝0，解得<i>m</i>＝2或<i>m</i>＝－1(舍).</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;存在正整数<i>m</i>＝2，使得<i>b</i><sub>m</sub>＋8＝<i>b</i><sub>m＋2</sub>－<i>b</i><sub>m＋1</sub>成立．</p>
</p><br>

<h1>2021级高二寒假数学作业8 等比数列</h1>

<h2>多选题</h2>

<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/2c178dc2bf404af9abbba4aab4b59c92.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    由题可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/1fa1f6613c164072b5123f090aef0e3f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>而<i>q</i>&gt;1，解得<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>所以<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝2<sup>n</sup>，即<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝log<sub>2</sub><i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝<i>n</i>，所以<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/976dab12e2884ceb9c4d118d75813069.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em"> 8 </p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    因为等比数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}，所以<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>·<i>a</i><sub>5</sub>＝<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>·<i>a</i><sub>6</sub>＝4.又<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>＋<i>a</i><sub>5</sub>＝5，<i>q</i>∈(0，1)，所以<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>＝4，<i>a</i><sub>5</sub>＝1，所以<i>q</i><sup>2</sup>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/3749e0f410a240a68ff0f1a068c81085.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<i>q</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/481fc3af89af4220a44e4c803978f023.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝4×(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/5cb6197c8ef14906bcaeb78a361e3d23.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>)<sup>n－3</sup>＝(<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/e57b70020e6c4422b421916329e49ab6.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>)<sup>n－5</sup>，所以<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝log<sub>2</sub><i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝5－<i>n</i>，易得数列{<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>}为等差数列，故<i>S</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/e588cbf5126d4403a3ca4a0e57ecbf29.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>.若<i>S</i><sub>n</sub>＞0，则0＜<i>n</i>＜9.因为<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>，所以<i>n</i>的最大值为8.</p>
</p><br>

<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    设等差数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}的公差为<i>d</i>，则<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/a2ee321c4fa249d3909518a9ed00564a.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>解得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/997447bb358246d1a37b1617733a3bdc.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝2＋2(<i>n</i>－1)＝2<i>n</i>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    由(1)知<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝|2<sup>n</sup>－32|，则</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    <i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/a5efa2a21deb46f3b68cf2adbe73a6aa.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    则<i>T</i><sub>10</sub>＝(<i>b</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>b</i><sub>2</sub>＋…＋<i>b</i><sub>5</sub>)＋(<i>b</i><sub>6</sub>＋<i>b</i><sub>7</sub>＋…＋<i>b</i><sub>10</sub>)
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ＝[32×5－(2<sup>1</sup>＋2<sup>2</sup>＋…＋2<sup>5</sup>)]＋[(2<sup>6</sup>＋2<sup>7</sup>＋…＋2<sup>10</sup>)－32×5]</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ＝－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/13ffc68ef5da49559940601ddd226dcb.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/c54a3f6928d944d0a48ecf90bb989095.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝(－2＋64)×31＝1 922.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1)
    由题，令<i>m</i>＝<i>n</i>＝1，得<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＝<i>a</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/e5510a34b93549c6a95bb06ccea4cead.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    又<i>S</i><sub>2</sub>＝<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＝12，解得<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝3或<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝－4(舍去)，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    则<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>＝9.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    令<i>m</i>＝1，得<i>a</i><sub>n＋1</sub>＝<i>a</i><sub>1</sub><i>a</i><sub>n</sub>，所以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/4f355278fc3f4e4f8de5a15c4216e4ac.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝3，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}是以3为首项、3为公比的等比数列，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝3<sup>n</sup>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(2)
    由(1)可得<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝<i>na</i><sub>n</sub>＝<i>n</i>·3<sup>n</sup>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝1×3<sup>1</sup>＋2×3<sup>2</sup>＋3×3<sup>3</sup>＋…＋<i>n</i>·3<sup>n</sup>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以3<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝1×3<sup>2</sup>＋2×3<sup>3</sup>＋3×3<sup>4</sup>＋…＋<i>n</i>·3<sup>n＋1</sup>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    两式相减，得－2<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝3<sup>1</sup>＋3<sup>2</sup>＋3<sup>3</sup>＋…＋3<sup>n</sup>－<i>n</i>·3<sup>n＋1</sup>，即－2<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/94f65883d27944dc93ab7a5304b1bba1.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>－<i>n</i>·3<sup>n＋1</sup>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以－2<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/8c6ba78b5cd947f98bffbc60056580a7.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    所以<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/718f651095d945efbb2f3f7f463fd048.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>

<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">(1) ∵
    2<i>S</i><sub>n</sub>＝(2<i>n</i>＋1)<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>－2<i>n</i><sup>2</sup>(<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>)，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;当<i>n</i>＝1时，2<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝3<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>－2，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝2；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    当<i>n</i>≥2时，由<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/9a933289c29448fe9b17d88b3709b8d9.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    得2<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝(2<i>n</i>＋1)<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>－(2<i>n</i>－1)<i>a</i><sub>n－1</sub>－2<i>n</i><sup>2</sup>＋2(<i>n</i>－1)<sup>2</sup>，即<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>－<i>a</i><sub>n－1</sub>＝2，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}是公差为2的等差数列．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">∵
    <i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝2，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝2<i>n</i>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    由条件得<i>b</i><sub>1</sub>＝2，<i>nb</i><sub>n＋1</sub>＝2<i>nb</i><sub>n</sub>，∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>b</i><sub>n＋1</sub>＝2<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>，即数列{<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>}是公比为2的等比数列，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>b</i><sub>n</sub>＝2<sup>n</sup>.</p>

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/6acae68fea0a4c1e85afc4599ab528ba.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img

        style="height:66px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>－<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝2－<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>＝4－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/400109432a694200af427f760479cdb7.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<i>λ</i>＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/0d6bea74b03c4e1883b6ab7ca7de0302.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>≥4－<i>T</i><sub>n</sub>(<i>n</i>∈N<sup>*</sup>)恒成立，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    则<i>λ</i>≥4－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/4b6ed456ae554d6d926c7dd87fb0815e.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>－4＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/41ee84b88df64fecbe63573d950e0540.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/dccec728aee746e8ac2f5aa582700317.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>恒成立．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    令<i>f</i>(<i>n</i>)＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/89c3ab6019d249ca8b4ac326e63cfafe.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，则<i>f</i>(<i>n</i>＋1)－<i>f</i>(<i>n</i>)＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/df6c1a6c1bc34d4da5396e54cd22f288.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/43301e7477794aeba525c0d657983a7d.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>f</i>(1)＜<i>f</i>(2)＜…＜<i>f</i>(6)＝<i>f</i>(7)＞<i>f</i>(8)＞…，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>f</i>(<i>n</i>)<sub>max</sub>＝<i>f</i>(6)＝<i>f</i>(7)＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/499c0675ee0848328b55faae2eff9a79.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>

    ∴&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>λ</i>≥<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/245bed8c940248d0ae76badd057f02c2.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;text-indent:2em">
    故实数<i>λ</i>的取值范围是[<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/7fb9c32a91f9423d8075433dee27e644/bffd22620b3b4e2a843282852d1891f9.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，＋∞).</p>

<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">6．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设等比数列的公比为<i>q</i>，由<i>a</i><sub>3</sub>+<i>a</i><sub>15</sub>＝12，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    可得<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/2dd9a01acb504468bba830740d03e869.png?"
        style="width:22px;height:47px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>+<i>a</i><sub>9</sub><i>q</i><sup>6</sup>＝12，则<i>a</i><sub>9</sub>＝<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/3cc0567f79b84a8aa9c79322bfb8c5d8.png?"
        style="width:53px;height:61px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由基本不等式得<i>q</i><sup>6</sup>+<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/e96b6fabda604597a87a3b29d9beb14d.png?"
        style="width:22px;height:42px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>≥2<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/5656fc41e5014a7ab2411cce79268be0.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>＝2，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    当且仅当<i>q</i><sup>6</sup>＝<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/3bacc9b30a5340a0a1538e36f0825397.png?"
        style="width:22px;height:42px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，即<i>q</i>＝±1时等号成立，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    所以<i>q</i><sup>6</sup>+<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/3ec16680932b46d4a29f5df1aae8a150.png?"
        style="width:22px;height:42px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>的最小值是2，所以当<i>q</i>＝±1时，<i>a</i><sub>9</sub>的最大值为6．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    ：<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezymath.alicdn.zykj.org/math?block=%5Cleft%5C%7B%5Cbegin%7Bmatrix%7D1(n%3D1)%5C%5C%5Cfrac%7Bn%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B(n-1)%5E%7B2%7D%7D(n%5Cgeq+2)%5Cend%7Bmatrix%7D%5Cright."
        style="display:inline-block"
        data-latex="\left\{\begin{matrix}1(n=1)\\\frac{n^{2}}{(n-1)^{2}}(n\geq 2)\end{matrix}\right."
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    在数列{<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>}中，<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>＝1，且<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>•<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>•…•<i>a</i><sub>n</sub>＝<i>n</i><sup>2</sup>，•••①
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    可得<i>a</i><sub>1</sub>•<i>a</i><sub>2</sub>•…•<i>a</i><sub>n﹣1</sub>＝（<i>n</i>﹣1）<sup>2</sup>（<i>n</i>≥2），•••②，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezymath.alicdn.zykj.org/math?block=%5Cfrac%7B%E2%91%A1%7D%7B%E2%91%A0%7D"
        style="display:inline-block" data-latex="\frac{②}{①}"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>可得<i>n</i>≥2时，<i>a</i><sub>n</sub><span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezymath.alicdn.zykj.org/math?block=%3D%5Cfrac%7Bn%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B(n-1)%5E%7B2%7D%7D"
        style="display:inline-block" data-latex="=\frac{n^{2}}{(n-1)^{2}}" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <span>​</span><span>​</span><img

<p><strong>04.</strong>

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    因为等差数列<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/dd32d56ac01a42b8939a2b96f6513465/9c4b4efe98a042578f9a9ed8bd1f9e99.png?"

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>满足<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">2021</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    已知函数<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>）在定义域（0，+∞）上是单调函数，且对任意<i>x</i>∈（0，+∞），都有<i>f</i>[<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>）﹣<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/5c96c6f44b1a40a6b8805e62f98fc299.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>]＝2，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    可设<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>）﹣<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/5c96c6f44b1a40a6b8805e62f98fc299.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:36px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>＝<i>c</i>，故<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>）＝<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/5c96c6f44b1a40a6b8805e62f98fc299.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:36px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>+<i>c</i>，且<i>f</i>（<i>c</i>）＝<i>c</i>+<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/f0571f5b91af46fe8a9caefeda56d47c.png?"
        style="width:13px;height:35px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>＝2（<i>c</i>＞0），解可得<i>c</i>＝1，<i>f</i>（<i>x</i>）＝<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/5c96c6f44b1a40a6b8805e62f98fc299.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>+1，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    则<i>f</i>（<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/8a2307e8544e4aeb835e31cc7bdab21f.png?"
        style="width:35px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>）＝2021．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故答案为：2021</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/25d4351509454c4d9d14ab2eea271ff6.png?"

    作出函数<i>f</i>(<i>x</i>)的图象，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/5d043abdbb4e46c9929401c5aec1293c.png?"

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>单调递减，且最小值为<i>f</i>(－1)＝－1，则令<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/b5c7ffd2ef924b1586610ed44fce9430.png?"

    故答案为：<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/25d4351509454c4d9d14ab2eea271ff6.png?"

<p><strong>03.</strong>

<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/94cb9479b05b42cc9070e469dad477a2.png?"
        style="width:140px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>（2）2</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【分析】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）将点带入，即可求解.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）问题转化为<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/cc8a715099444cea82c52c6c09000d9d.png?"
        style="width:95px;height:36px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/72cf145396a44e568d4aa8534b37c704.png?"
        style="width:30px;height:23px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>上有解，求出函数<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/2a81b06dfadc48ddaab46c155a5d507c.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>的最小值，即可求解.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）由题意<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/95f6ec3dc4584f12afecc704581ce5d0.png?"
        style="width:106px;height:46px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>解得<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/bdb599c606f34066801670df6ed806d1.png?"
        style="width:49px;height:42px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>所以<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/94cb9479b05b42cc9070e469dad477a2.png?"
        style="width:140px;height:39px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）由（1），<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/cc8a715099444cea82c52c6c09000d9d.png?"
        style="width:95px;height:36px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/72cf145396a44e568d4aa8534b37c704.png?"
        style="width:30px;height:23px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>上有解，则<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/79a92e6447634435b6e35dc3b6982dc9.png?"
        style="width:95px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    函数<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/2a81b06dfadc48ddaab46c155a5d507c.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:36px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/72cf145396a44e568d4aa8534b37c704.png?"
        style="width:30px;height:23px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>严格单调递增，所以当<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/d58a254534234ed0b5fe1e5c085ecc76.png?"
        style="width:30px;height:16px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>时，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/2a81b06dfadc48ddaab46c155a5d507c.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>取最小值2．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    所以<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/4d636b0b75e14ed2ba891cc7d3f679f6.png?"
        style="width:29px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，即：<i>t</i>的最小值为2．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）当<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/7213db3e72e047698a9fd0dcfa5050bb.png?"
        style="width:30px;height:17px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>时，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/e617fce9f9af4e79abd773d142d1083e.png?"
        style="width:104px;height:24px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/6a605003c11c4289bd427cdad16e2dcd.png?"
        style="width:53px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由二次函数的性质可得<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/e617fce9f9af4e79abd773d142d1083e.png?"
        style="width:104px;height:24px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/84d8264055d44fd492b849542245d8ad/771e7bc5c5f54f5d896f00b1108a4707.png?"
        style="width:29px;height:24px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>上单调递减，在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

    解：根据题意，可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/bbb549f6822942ef914b35c374d2eb35.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/4863ff78f6ee43ea8261b3763737d341.png?"

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解：依据题意，可知<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/df42e1db36424babbc14f1543cba295a.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/a91fb3e484864603ba1526a060c51f12.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/ab509ad42fc04e2ba45f0ed6cd3543ce.png?"

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">所以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/52f0d992c87d46d487cc7267e87f2d8c.png?"

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（Ⅱ）由上知，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/fd529222d33447fcaab29019a63cdeec/ba23125335fe49c5a0f96b35a32534d8.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:18px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为第二象限的角，</p>

</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）连接<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/2376066eb08c46cab007d88f748ae132/cf9b11f33abf42398b1cbdedbd51c728.png?"
        style="width:21px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>交<span>​</span><img

        style="width:27px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>于<span>​</span><img

        style="width:14px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，进而证明<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/2376066eb08c46cab007d88f748ae132/2826c2b62ae24aa9a509540b4ad62591.png?"
        style="width:62px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，然后根据线面平行的判定定理证明问题；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）建立空间直角坐标系，求出平面<span>​</span><img

        style="width:34px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的法向量，进而通过空间向量的夹角公式求得答案；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（3）求出平面<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/2376066eb08c46cab007d88f748ae132/5326a9b6aae445e3a12e4c91188ebcf2.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的法向量，结合（2），进而通过空间向量的夹角公式求得答案.</p>

<p><strong>03.</strong>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由已知条件可得椭圆的标准方程是<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由已知条件得椭圆的焦点在<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:49px;height:20px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:29px;height:14px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，从而<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:29px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，</p>

    ∴其标准方程是：<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/0c2296b3ea4b461dafb513732722405a/740732ed499f41ae8efd3aca45a2d319.png?"
        style="width:59px;height:34px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，</p>

    联立方程组<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/0c2296b3ea4b461dafb513732722405a/4616afacd08e4fd8a440a64cde7578e3.png?"

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，消去<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>得，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:112px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">

<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）证明见解析</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）存在</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）利用勾股定理证得<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/0c2296b3ea4b461dafb513732722405a/25fabac82fcf4edc909f751a47e14b06.png?"
        style="width:57px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，结合线面垂直的判定定理即可证得结论；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）以<i>A</i>为原点建立空间直角坐标系，设点<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:33px;height:16px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>的法向量<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:13px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>的方程，进而得解.</p>

<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/0c2296b3ea4b461dafb513732722405a/97630ea3cb3b4ef28e5ca835973a1699.png?"

        style="width:63px;height:32px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，即求；</p>

        style="width:173px;height:45px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>判断数列的单调性，即得.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>

    由题可设<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        style="width:16px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>成等差数列，</p>

    则<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/0c2296b3ea4b461dafb513732722405a/05d02f01a5ac408ca793ffbd1d690782.png?"

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，即<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

    ∴<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><span>​</span><img

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>
