<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7e35cc04a1584330bac5c8bb451ed915.png?"
        style="width:83px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">利用空间向量的线性运算即得.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    ∵<i>D</i>为<i>BC</i>的中点，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6040353276c344d1b9e4cda05e9f685f.png?"
        style="width:135px;height:23px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，点<i>E</i>为<i>AD</i>中点，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d81b61a8b0314d719fbe16cc611b713b.png?"
        style="width:197px;height:211px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c274a48735484c4ebc77221df6c70995.png?"
        style="width:484px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故答案为：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7e35cc04a1584330bac5c8bb451ed915.png?"
        style="width:83px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2127f17b879b416c9aa28a63d86788b0.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">计算故以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a34a3effe1d14d4ab421ea7f03690487.png?"
        style="width:13px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为圆心，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a762d8328d4e4974800556c7c79ceacd.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为半径的圆方程，两圆方程相减得到答案.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8bee56e4470243bda53c6eb3bbc6c80e.png?"
        style="width:265px;height:31px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a34a3effe1d14d4ab421ea7f03690487.png?"
        style="width:13px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为圆心，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a762d8328d4e4974800556c7c79ceacd.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为半径的圆为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/aff5da1e4a6341e7b1e567ce2dc390d1.png?"
        style="width:124px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    两圆方程相减得到<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2127f17b879b416c9aa28a63d86788b0.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>即为直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/f611cb84af7945779fac5e0e9ee90bb1.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>方程.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故答案为：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2127f17b879b416c9aa28a63d86788b0.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ee207e1c7caa416aaf0fd199559520de.png?"
        style="width:31px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">设点<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a34a3effe1d14d4ab421ea7f03690487.png?"
        style="width:13px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为第一象限内的点，设椭圆与双曲线的焦点都在<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/00e46d3e211a44b9b7e8f11358c961c1.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>轴上，设椭圆的长轴长为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/10375b50f59f40b5a60a1e99657b0cdd.png?"
        style="width:21px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，双曲线的实轴长为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/19a7f55a9a8845e1979e55b35bfed995.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，两曲线的焦距为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7e6d4da6bc8c458d900efbe351b3f1fa.png?"
        style="width:16px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，椭圆和双曲线的离心率分别为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c582ab16234846a29f6e690a38c0e190.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/4359644e336c49cdaac4df72e702ebb3.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，利用余弦定理、椭圆和双曲线的定义可得出<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a5430a5b3df943f7840cf7c671577843.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:23px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，进而可得出<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d753bf9444db4c598c5fd64ebc528377.png?"
        style="width:67px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，结合<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/cabe1901a7574d19b232346c195c350d.png?"
        style="width:47px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>可求得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/4359644e336c49cdaac4df72e702ebb3.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的值，即可得解.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设椭圆与双曲线的焦点都在<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/00e46d3e211a44b9b7e8f11358c961c1.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>轴上，设椭圆的长轴长为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/10375b50f59f40b5a60a1e99657b0cdd.png?"
        style="width:21px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，双曲线的实轴长为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/19a7f55a9a8845e1979e55b35bfed995.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，两曲线的焦距为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7e6d4da6bc8c458d900efbe351b3f1fa.png?"
        style="width:16px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，椭圆和双曲线的离心率分别为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c582ab16234846a29f6e690a38c0e190.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/4359644e336c49cdaac4df72e702ebb3.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">不妨设<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a34a3effe1d14d4ab421ea7f03690487.png?"
        style="width:13px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为第一象限的点，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ff646002756347ada4a6f96b70e7854d.png?"
        style="width:432px;height:143px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">在椭圆中：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7672c488d7584fcdb4ac22ad312a2037.png?"
        style="width:89px;height:20px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>①，在双曲线中：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/58a0c8b29eec4fd0a84a570072b4919f.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:20px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>②，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">联立①②解得，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/bf6a044948f746eeba25c833e9471e73.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:20px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8cc95e9721834ef78a3af8460c922f60.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:20px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">在<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/f04f4aed88684b3ea5d9d32f71718fc5.png?"
        style="width:49px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>中由余弦定理得：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/475c2d80e1234dfc95c90d432a49c3ce.png?"
        style="width:238px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2e153af246704b459d2015db7d1b71a0.png?"
        style="width:291px;height:37px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1b8510f99f3844cfae58cb002fdf92e8.png?"
        style="width:218px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/53370a8d5b9046bf9271ecd345f2eb62.png?"
        style="width:76px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d753bf9444db4c598c5fd64ebc528377.png?"
        style="width:67px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    因为椭圆的离心率<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/cabe1901a7574d19b232346c195c350d.png?"
        style="width:47px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以双曲线的离心率<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/af03db6c4fce4f86877584ba8bb6d8cf.png?"
        style="width:56px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故答案为：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ee207e1c7caa416aaf0fd199559520de.png?"
        style="width:31px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【点睛】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">方法点睛：求解椭圆或双曲线的离心率的方法如下：
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）定义法：通过已知条件列出方程组，求得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/31c3cdae71c74c02bb9717b95180054a.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:13px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2e9b9dfd31d54c49bf3f9802de3292e3.png?"
        style="width:11px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的值，根据离心率的定义求解离心率<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c819f95d2e584e82a5f6fd2e3e567e04.png?"
        style="width:9px;height:12px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的值；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）齐次式法：由已知条件得出关于<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/31c3cdae71c74c02bb9717b95180054a.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:13px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/2e9b9dfd31d54c49bf3f9802de3292e3.png?"
        style="width:11px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的齐次方程，然后转化为关于<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c819f95d2e584e82a5f6fd2e3e567e04.png?"
        style="width:9px;height:12px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程求解；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （3）特殊值法：通过取特殊位置或特殊值，求得离心率.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8de22cc0d9aa40f6b0604bea20151151.png?"
        style="width:37px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">做出曲线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ea98ef9c82064b3eb77f65b0b8466121.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:27px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的图象，结合直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1c31f88a38cc4fc5860c3f24cc94e62a.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>过定点<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/99ab1f7d39fd4202a6eb01b84ce0a5c3.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，数形结合即可求出结果.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由题意可知，曲线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ea98ef9c82064b3eb77f65b0b8466121.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:27px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>表示圆心为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/35e69928cbc74666971d4b27e3d1227b.png?"
        style="width:42px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，半径为1的圆的上半部分（含端点），则直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1c31f88a38cc4fc5860c3f24cc94e62a.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>与曲线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ea98ef9c82064b3eb77f65b0b8466121.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:27px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>有两个不同的公共点时，且直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1c31f88a38cc4fc5860c3f24cc94e62a.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>过定点<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/99ab1f7d39fd4202a6eb01b84ce0a5c3.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/fbc154cdc63b47f1b2d737b247f06d6f.png?"
        style="width:216px;height:192px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    可考虑临界状态，即直线与半圆相切时或直线经过点<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/dbc3b94ea4294bfc82fb577e25250c85.png?"
        style="width:44px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">当过点<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/dbc3b94ea4294bfc82fb577e25250c85.png?"
        style="width:44px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>时，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/236470a5a0194a26bb03a8026bd2b64c.png?"
        style="width:89px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/f73f3beeedb74863a5b282acf47b2f67.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">当直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1c31f88a38cc4fc5860c3f24cc94e62a.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>与圆相切时，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/b5989aa501bc41e1a7b389363082dd98.png?"
        style="width:87px;height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3bb2ef1b0bef4d668db4e2f708f20f36.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:33px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    数形结合可知有两个不同的公共点时实数<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7ff4bcef9fbc4cd1960789d699b6af31.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的取值范围为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8de22cc0d9aa40f6b0604bea20151151.png?"
        style="width:37px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故答案为：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8de22cc0d9aa40f6b0604bea20151151.png?"
        style="width:37px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>

<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/b94b4aa0127e4e4e8a88efe2a7569866.png?"
        style="width:93px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>（2）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/395ab6541e664b23911183c38ff942c6.png?"
        style="width:32px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>或<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/30ec71c97e5f479ea0a33d974c265e00.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）设出圆的半径，根据圆的弦长公式可求出半径，即可写出圆<i>C</i>的标准方程；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）当斜率不存在时，检验是符合；当斜率存在时，由点斜式设出直线方程，根据直线与圆相切，即可求出斜率，得到直线方程．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）根据题意，设圆C的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/de23c5a8d1af41aa85df0f411f844ef7.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">因为圆C被直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8897d8128ed64e0c8122e479ccd5fcfc.png?"
        style="width:88px;height:23px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>截得的弦长为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ff6f232832464eda9c72f5a181d21489.png?"
        style="width:28px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，圆心<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/10769c0356554433aa98363aa303851f.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>到直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8897d8128ed64e0c8122e479ccd5fcfc.png?"
        style="width:88px;height:23px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的距离为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/37de194f998c42f0aa55ee030a702072.png?"
        style="width:84px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，则<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/1c153ad2c00d481199b1baab6ed71c2a.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/72186eaa3fbb40c7a79681adc9e41584.png?"
        style="width:33px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    则圆C的标准方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/b94b4aa0127e4e4e8a88efe2a7569866.png?"
        style="width:93px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）当斜率不存在时，直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/395ab6541e664b23911183c38ff942c6.png?"
        style="width:32px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">显然圆心<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/9c6e8279084c4e23a01bb59453bac3bf.png?"
        style="width:29px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>到<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/395ab6541e664b23911183c38ff942c6.png?"
        style="width:32px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的距离为3，正好等于半径，符合题意；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    当斜率存在时，设斜率为k，则过M点的直线方程为：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3fb3880349934f8393ca7263e7a60809.png?"
        style="width:89px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/225fca82f4ab4dfdb79a7b346ed71e2b.png?"
        style="width:103px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，圆心到直线的距离等于半径3，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/78f2ff29dd274f23b0ab6439e5a6a800.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/05d6d583d79f4d72b80999258a47860e.png?"
        style="width:40px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">所以直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/30ec71c97e5f479ea0a33d974c265e00.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    综上，所求的直线方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/395ab6541e664b23911183c38ff942c6.png?"
        style="width:32px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>或<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/30ec71c97e5f479ea0a33d974c265e00.png?"
        style="width:99px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【点睛】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    本题主要考查圆的方程求法以及直线与圆的位置关系的应用，注意分类讨论思想的应用，属于基础题．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）证明见解析；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/956034c839494e8792e3352a0eac6a36.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/b6c04fc325bb49ca9701e12ac350bc63.png?"
        style="width:42px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【分析】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）由题设可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ca47e37125184677bf8ea1a130de9866.png?"
        style="width:73px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即可证明结论；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）由（1）可知<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/246b1fa037fb4f0fa275d49582a92db6.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，再根据<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3aee4646be914731a920a549bec5b393.png?"
        style="width:120px;height:45px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>计算可得；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/9647f95d42ed4365ae7c7941d06f11e3.png?"
        style="width:36px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/5adff3a61e43410c871db039f8252e9a.png?"
        style="width:162px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/05c1d53635fb4428942727e2c54afc6e.png?"
        style="width:110px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，整理得：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ca47e37125184677bf8ea1a130de9866.png?"
        style="width:73px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，而<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/22e90ab794834307b25d169cb255424b.png?"
        style="width:64px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c1a60ddab54f49af99c94abc17ea835c.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d6b36a5e421b40c2a7de12d28bd4ef48.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为首项，1为公差的等差数列，得证.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由（1）得：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/246b1fa037fb4f0fa275d49582a92db6.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">①当<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6a7611c033a54b42be7e8e20422fcfad.png?"
        style="width:31px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>时，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c0040d01d9b845008a039ec118e051eb.png?"
        style="width:63px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">②当<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/c8e113bbec694e58ba9dd9ae11668168.png?"

        style="width:92px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>成立，</p>

        style="width:42px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）证明见解析；（2）<span>​</span><img

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">

    （3）根据（2）中平面<span>​</span><img

        style="width:45px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的距离．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">【详解】</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解：（1）证明：连接<i>BE</i>，<i>BF</i>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/b05d4b7ba32e449395ec6741dc05e4b2.png?"

        style="width:28px;height:23px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>

        style="width:14px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，连接<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/19882667671444f59fdf539ecd3aa0ea.png?"
        style="width:24px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img

<p><strong>04.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8a1756983ba04bb495a64a6525f1a2ab.png?"
        style="width:41px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）偶函数，证明见解析；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（3）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/fe7be33f9a0c4855a4b67c1f425cad11.png?"
        style="width:65px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>或<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/dd8dd1ddf1154ece82dfd0feea515276.png?"
        style="width:54px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）由对数的性质列不等式组求<i>x</i>的范围，即可得<i>y</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a8b8bafc240e466da1a11a3de7bda116.png?"
        style="width:28px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>定义域；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）根据函数奇偶性的定义判断<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a8b8bafc240e466da1a11a3de7bda116.png?"
        style="width:28px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的奇偶性；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（3）化简函数<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/a8b8bafc240e466da1a11a3de7bda116.png?"
        style="width:28px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的解析式为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/0c72bd59d330413ea964fe9b9825b411.png?"
        style="width:104px;height:25px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，结合已知及函数的奇偶性及区间单调性可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ee7c0085da3f4a7a9ba36d5ce98c2d37.png?"
        style="width:94px;height:67px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，由此求得<i>m</i>的范围．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由对数的性质知：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/dc49a5a497e84d518f209b93ff6f820b.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:42px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e8627cf68641457683484d780fd04bc9.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6b89b1b1cb9e41579c1ccaa7b900e383.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的定义域为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/8a1756983ba04bb495a64a6525f1a2ab.png?"
        style="width:41px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/fd58cc93ec3c4041aed0eff3d651efe1.png?"
        style="width:211px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，结合（1）所得的定义域，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6b89b1b1cb9e41579c1ccaa7b900e383.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>偶函数.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（3）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∵<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/46c2f5a9943742e984e9d60f5a00af62.png?"
        style="width:231px;height:25px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6b89b1b1cb9e41579c1ccaa7b900e383.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>是[0,3<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/458a3d2d074449508ce26307cb501c4e.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:18px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>上的减函数，又<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6b89b1b1cb9e41579c1ccaa7b900e383.png?"
        style="width:34px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>是偶函数.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ee7c0085da3f4a7a9ba36d5ce98c2d37.png?"
        style="width:94px;height:67px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/fe7be33f9a0c4855a4b67c1f425cad11.png?"
        style="width:65px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>或<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/dd8dd1ddf1154ece82dfd0feea515276.png?"
        style="width:54px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>05.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/bf9cefc430724964b617df28f203ace7.png?"
        style="width:66px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/f07ed75d90704543b0c4912bfda84315.png?"
        style="width:68px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）根据已知条件可得出关于<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/31c3cdae71c74c02bb9717b95180054a.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:13px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d39712f56c7a4b6aa82d0da68612cf15.png?"
        style="width:12px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/0029f8f4004e49e3939aae4d689ee4cf.png?"
        style="width:11px;height:14px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程组，解出这三个量的值，即可得出椭圆<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3101a66da22d488ea6e0baae6ce6be86.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）由直线与圆相切可得出<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6f4765559e0b45fa931268a7b2410c2b.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:26px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，将直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>的方程与椭圆方程联立，列出韦达定理，利用平面向量数量积的坐标运算结合韦达定理计算得出<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d5173f4e5876405ca200541122618710.png?"
        style="width:69px;height:20px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即可求得结果.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解：由已知可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ba07b896ee784c9483e6861c5487312f.png?"
        style="width:82px;height:122px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/16bb59e2ed384b298ed68254ebad5072.png?"
        style="width:52px;height:72px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，故椭圆<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3101a66da22d488ea6e0baae6ce6be86.png?"
        style="width:14px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/bf9cefc430724964b617df28f203ace7.png?"
        style="width:66px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解：因为直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>与圆<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/545d8c0d334e4947845082a364e4b880.png?"
        style="width:68px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>相切，且直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d1ce5c78a2094166b39d762bb213cd16.png?"
        style="width:56px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">所以<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/12bdd8ff5a644c87a24a4d52dc3ded4f.png?"
        style="width:80px;height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/6f4765559e0b45fa931268a7b2410c2b.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:26px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">联立<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/3af3d554acea4591a4f7b44dbd01fcdb.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:62px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，整理得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/5471785bc4ee4c77aebe83375f553577.png?"
        style="width:189px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/31dcdf0478694c2c961f9226a7fe49f7.png?"
        style="width:216px;height:26px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">设<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/69154c6dc74946629383a6330ac92438.png?"

        style="width:56px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，则<span>​</span><img

        style="width:93px;height:33px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img

        style="width:86px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/827a4556630a45449aeb58e16775359d.png?"
        style="width:364px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">则<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/0e78fdadcc3e4884ac50001ab7298c0e.png?"
        style="width:351px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，故<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/f07ed75d90704543b0c4912bfda84315.png?"
        style="width:68px;height:36px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>

<p><strong>06.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/09b8f8c3c43343639814054d8a0a48bc.png?"
        style="width:64px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （2）存在，直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/64a5d1e9d60a497fbfe823fd4031b1dc.png?"
        style="width:31px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>或<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/7bffc912374b47d69d54da53949bd27b.png?"
        style="width:92px;height:17px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    （1）根据焦距、双曲线上的点求双曲线参数，进而写出双曲线<i>C</i>的方程；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）由题设有<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/316558bb0eaf43d1bd7b5fddc14cef6b.png?"
        style="width:40px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，设直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d9b54d407b1b44b5bfd4a3d16796bb70.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:37px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/d2158d8c8bf14915b7f250ab56694a8e.png?"
        style="width:104px;height:19px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，并联立双曲线方程，应用韦达定理、中点坐标公式求<i>M</i>，<i>N</i>的中点坐标，由等腰三角形中垂线性质求参数<i>k</i>，进而可得直线<i>l</i>的方程.
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（1）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由题设，<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/28798ec36b5e497ab1603ee81ab3b90f.png?"
        style="width:44px;height:21px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，又<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/48b056089676452a9f5b122fc2149db4.png?"
        style="width:60px;height:24px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>在双曲线上，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">∴<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/62fdc1695c434221b685b5b9090cc73e.png?"
        style="width:72px;height:63px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，可得<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/ca12b934b4f741c5bd4ccb490737cb84.png?"
        style="width:45px;height:46px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    ∴双曲线<i>C</i>的方程为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/09b8f8c3c43343639814054d8a0a48bc.png?"
        style="width:64px;height:40px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">（2）</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由（1）知：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/316558bb0eaf43d1bd7b5fddc14cef6b.png?"
        style="width:40px;height:19px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>的斜率一定存在，当直线斜率为0时，直线<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/e994c0fd197b411a82dad7a8341507a1.png?"
        style="width:8px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>：<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/63248e0dfe154a2f9496cdc8ed5f6ecc/64a5d1e9d60a497fbfe823fd4031b1dc.png?"
        style="width:31px;height:16px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，符合题意；</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">设直线<span>​</span><img

<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业1 动量定理及应用</h1>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>A</p><br>

<p><strong>07.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>08.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>09.</strong>A</p><br>
<p><strong>10.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>11.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>12.</strong>C</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 12 s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 解法一 用动量定理，分段求解．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    选物体为研究对象，对于撤去<i>F</i>前物体做匀加速运动的过程，始态速度为零，终态速度为<i>v</i>.取水平力<i>F</i>的方向为正方向，根据动量定理有(<i>F</i>－<i>μmg</i>)<i>t</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>mv</i>－0，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    对于撤去<i>F</i>后物体做匀减速运动的过程，始态速度为<i>v</i>，终态速度为零．根据动量定理有－<i>μmgt</i><sub>2</sub>＝0－<i>mv</i>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    联立解得<i>t</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/f7762cf9e28e426d95161033578f291c/07b7d4ba46fd4f079c1b6ccde0bf81c4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>t</i><sub>1</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/f7762cf9e28e426d95161033578f291c/46993adfc5114218a293791896595b7a.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span
        style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">×</span>6 s＝12 s.
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解法二 用动量定理，研究全过程．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    选物体作为研究对象，研究整个运动过程，这个过程的始、末状态物体的速度都等于零．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    取水平力<i>F</i>的方向为正方向，根据动量定理得</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (<i>F</i>－<i>μmg</i>)<i>t</i><sub>1</sub>＋(－<i>μmg</i>)<i>t</i><sub>2</sub>＝0</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解得<i>t</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/f7762cf9e28e426d95161033578f291c/1f4a3d9a63c541c9b9ce7d528c1948a8.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>t</i><sub>1</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/f7762cf9e28e426d95161033578f291c/2658e20f36804297ab15e38b68c00633.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>×6 s＝12 s. </p>
</p><br>
<hr>

<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业2 动量守恒定律及应用</h1>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>A</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>05.</strong>A</p><br>
<p><strong>06.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>07.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>08.</strong>B</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)3.0 m/s (2)4.3 m/s
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)设<i>B</i>车的质量为<i>m</i><sub>B</sub>，碰后加速度大小为<i>a</i><sub>B</sub>.根据牛顿第二定律有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>μm</i><sub>B</sub><i>g</i>＝<i>m</i><sub>B</sub><i>a</i><sub>B</sub>①</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">式中<i>μ</i>是汽车与路面间的动摩擦因数．
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设碰撞后瞬间<i>B</i>车速度的大小为<i>v</i><sub>B</sub>′，碰撞后滑行的距离为<i>s</i><sub>B</sub>.由运动学公式有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>v</i><sub>B</sub>′<sup>2</sup>＝2<i>a</i><sub>B</sub><i>s</i><sub>B</sub>②</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">联立①②式并利用题给数据得</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>v</i><sub>B</sub>′＝3.0
    m/s③</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)设<i>A</i>车的质量为<i>m</i><sub>A</sub>，碰后加速度大小为<i>a</i><sub>A</sub>，根据牛顿第二定律有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>μm</i><sub>A</sub><i>g</i>＝<i>m</i><sub>A</sub><i>a</i><sub>A</sub>④</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设碰撞后瞬间<i>A</i>车速度的大小为<i>v</i><sub>A</sub>′，碰撞后滑行的距离为<i>s</i><sub>A</sub>，由运动学公式有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>v</i><sub>A</sub>′<sup>2</sup>＝2<i>a</i><sub>A</sub><i>s</i><sub>A</sub>⑤</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设碰撞前的瞬间<i>A</i>车速度的大小为<i>v</i><sub>A</sub>.两车在碰撞过程中动量守恒，有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>m</i><sub>A</sub><i>v</i><sub>A</sub>＝<i>m</i><sub>A</sub><i>v</i><sub>A</sub>′＋<i>m</i><sub>B</sub><i>v</i><sub>B</sub>′⑥
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">联立③④⑤⑥式并利用题给数据得</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>v</i><sub>A</sub>≈4.3
    m/s.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 大于或等于3.8 m/s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    人跳到乙车上后，如果两车同向，且甲车的速度等于乙车的速度就可以恰好避免两车相撞</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">以人、甲车、乙车组成的系统为研究对象，以向右为正方向
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由水平方向动量守恒得</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (<i>m</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>M</i>)<i>v</i>－<i>m</i><sub>2</sub><i>v</i><sub>0</sub>＝(<i>m</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>m</i><sub>2</sub>＋<i>M</i>)<i>v</i>′
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解得<i>v</i>′＝1 m/s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    以人与甲车为一系统，人跳离甲车过程水平方向动量守恒，得(<i>m</i><sub>1</sub>＋<i>M</i>)<i>v</i>＝<i>m</i><sub>1</sub><i>v</i>′＋<i>Mu</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解得<i>u</i>＝3.8 m/s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">因此，只要人跳离甲车的速度大于或等于3.8
    m/s，就可避免两车相撞．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)5.5 J (2)60 N (3)见解析
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)物块恰好通过<i>C</i>点，有<i>mg</i>＝<i>m</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/779c9496309e4b90afdf34c0a1bb3aee.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解得<i>v</i><sub>C</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/e6fb9f06baef44abb959426b3c98dbd2.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> m/s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由动能定理得，<i>W</i>－<i>μmgL</i><sub>0</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/443b1dc755874d9787ef62672b60140f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>mv</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/3eb479ad352748ea95f3cb3349e822bf.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解得<i>W</i>＝5.5 J</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)物块由<i>C</i>运动到<i>D</i>，由动能定理得2<i>mgR</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/6d92e0a99b0b4d9080e313bfd5598a88.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>mv</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/9dad1a51d1db46bba0a570a080391a50.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/11f6565771e54c34b50c1e935d6f05ef.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>mv</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/4dda534ffadc44e6a8257dcc6f75ed0c.png?"

    m/s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    在<i>D</i>点，<i>F</i>－<i>mg</i>＝<i>m</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/82d0d99b40af4077945ff4ed61e6f54e/cbbefa85b6404d5888c05146d1af2d37.png?"

    <i>mv</i><sub>D</sub>＝(<i>M</i>＋<i>m</i>)<i>v</i><sub>共</sub></p>

<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业3 机械振动</h1>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>C</p><br>

<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/09557beb8bfa48f7be9ce29bd1bd40c4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> (2)AC (3)乙 (4)AC (5)12.0 (6)BC
    (7)<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/790b995a5e124b71b6f8510476129c12.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/e419a4a43e214080a644df1c3b304281.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> (8)CD</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)单摆的周期<i>T</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/40a8278b65de43f9b98c6ab5d9049440.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，由单摆周期公式<i>T</i>＝2π<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/a810442efe894b039281d373547e9709.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>得重力加速度<i>g</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/6d618b30648447b5ae16e5407a82fbaf.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/09557beb8bfa48f7be9ce29bd1bd40c4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)为了便于测量周期和减小空气阻力，摆线选择较细且结实的线，故选A；为了减小空气阻力的影响，摆球选择质量大体积小的，故选C.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (3)为了避免运动过程中摆长发生变化，悬点要固定，不能松动，则选图乙．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (4)这样做的目的是便于调节摆长，把摆线夹得更紧一些，使摆动过程中摆长不变，因此A、C正确．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(5)摆球的直径为<i>d</i>＝12.0 mm.
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (6)摆长等于摆线的长度加上摆球的半径，A错误；将停表测量摆球完成一次全振动所用时间作为单摆的周期，误差较大，应采用累积法测量周期，D错误．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (7)根据单摆周期公式<i>T</i>＝2π<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/a810442efe894b039281d373547e9709.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/3be5598e633c43ff8391e1b52412be91.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/790b995a5e124b71b6f8510476129c12.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以应该作出<i>T</i>－<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/790b995a5e124b71b6f8510476129c12.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>图像，故横坐标所代表的物理量是<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/790b995a5e124b71b6f8510476129c12.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，斜率<i>k</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/3be5598e633c43ff8391e1b52412be91.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得<i>g</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/e419a4a43e214080a644df1c3b304281.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (8)由周期公式<i>T</i>＝2π<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/a810442efe894b039281d373547e9709.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，得<i>g</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/6d618b30648447b5ae16e5407a82fbaf.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，单摆振幅大小与<i>g</i>无关，故A错误；开始计时时，过早按下停表，周期偏大，则<i>g</i>偏小，故B错误；测量周期时，误将摆球(<i>n</i>－1)次全振动的时间记为<i>n</i>次全振动的时间，周期偏小，则<i>g</i>偏大，故C正确；摆长等于摆线的长度加上摆球的半径，若测量摆长时以悬点到小球下端边缘的距离为摆长，摆长偏大，由<i>g</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/6d618b30648447b5ae16e5407a82fbaf.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，所以<i>g</i>偏大，故D正确．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)0.5 0.64 (2)B (3)AC
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)根据题图(b)的信息可得，摆球第一次摆到最低点时，力传感器显示的力最大，所对应的时刻为<i>t</i>＝0.5 s．根据题图(b)的信息可得，单摆周期<i>T</i>＝1.6
    s，由单摆周期公式<i>T</i>＝2π<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/a810442efe894b039281d373547e9709.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得摆长为<i>l</i>＝0.64 m.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)单摆振动的回复力是摆球重力在垂直摆线方向上的分力，而摆球所受重力和摆线对摆球拉力的合力在径向上提供向心力，选项B正确．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (3)测得摆长应为<i>l</i>＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/308d5347dc9e4d0caa01cb1fbd1b17a4/48aa8b4d803d444e96f7f818db18f24f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>，选项B错误；若让小球在水平面内做圆周运动，则为圆锥摆运动，测得的摆动周期不是单摆运动周期，选项D错误．</p>
</p><br>
