<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业4 机械波</h1>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>05.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>06.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>07.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>08.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>09.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>10.</strong>C</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 2 m/s 0.8 m</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 由题图可知，周期<i>T</i>＝0.4 s
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由于波长大于0.6
    m，结合题图可知，波从<i>A</i>到<i>B</i>的传播时间Δ<i>t</i>＝0.3 s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    波速<i>v</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/4e2f9cc6ea1245a882615f6c22ace172/8cc22b2649034703b8d164115f9479a4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，代入数据得<i>v</i>＝2 m/s，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    波长<i>λ</i>＝<i>vT</i>，代入数据得<i>λ</i>＝0.8 m.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/4e2f9cc6ea1245a882615f6c22ace172/2876e77a228a46a598dc7fd399b1e4b4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>T</i>＝0.2 s</p>

<h2>填空题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 频率 <i>C</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    从两狭缝发出的光，它们的频率相同，在波峰与波谷相遇的区域中，振动相互抵消，会出现暗条纹，即在<i>C</i>点出现暗条纹．</p>

    解得<i>v</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/3899434fbb9845cb9247c97920c86f82.png?"

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)金属棒所受安培力<i>F</i><sub>安</sub>＝<i>IdB</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    金属棒所受合力<i>F</i>＝<i>mg</i>sin <i>θ</i>－<i>F</i><sub>安</sub></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由牛顿第二定律有<i>F</i>＝<i>ma</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解得<i>I</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/47cd810103524fd28bc23334c8a830ee.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (3)金属棒的运动时间<i>t</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/f12acb612a734686a726db090be44b4a.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">通过的电荷量<i>Q</i>＝<i>It</i>
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解得<i>Q</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/506b746c2a564cda92ee1254acbcd600.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(1)<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/bb6d9609ac8b4b76b2e771a76a96397d.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> N≤<i>F</i>≤8 N (2)0≤<i>R</i>≤30 Ω</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)当金属棒刚好达到向上运动的临界状态时，金属棒受到的摩擦力为最大静摩擦力，方向平行斜面向下，对金属棒受力分析，如图甲所示，此时金属棒所受安培力最大，设为<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>，则有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    垂直斜面方向：<i>F</i><sub>N</sub>＝<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>sin <i>θ</i>＋<i>mg</i>cos <i>θ</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    沿斜面方向：<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>cos <i>θ</i>＝<i>mg</i>sin <i>θ</i>＋<i>F</i><sub>fmax</sub></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    又<i>F</i><sub>fmax</sub>＝<i>μF</i><sub>N</sub></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    以上三式联立并代入数据可得<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>＝8 N</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/8c745f85c62d48449aba987ae486a9d5.png?"
        style="width:95px;height:84px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/5da1c6531d764e7db9cb13c52aca1809.png?"
        style="width:95px;height:100px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>当金属棒刚好达到向下运动的临界状态时，金属棒受到的摩擦力为最大静摩擦力，方向平行斜面向上，其受力分析如图乙所示，此时金属棒所受安培力最小，设为<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>，则有
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>F</i><sub>N</sub>′＝<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>sin <i>θ</i>＋<i>mg</i>cos <i>θ</i>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>F</i><sub>2</sub>cos
    <i>θ</i>＋<i>F</i><sub>fmax</sub>′＝<i>mg</i>sin <i>θ</i>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>F</i><sub>fmax</sub>′＝<i>μF</i><sub>N</sub>′</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    以上三式联立并代入数据可得<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/1e82ae9891ee4cd1a9ab4f8725c0cfa3.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> N</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    所以金属棒受到的安培力的取值范围为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/08cd99a2f1f74310b87e8d57c2b8dce4.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> N≤<i>F</i>≤8 N</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)因磁场与金属棒垂直，所以金属棒受到的安培力为<i>F</i>＝<i>BIL</i>，因此有<i>I</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/e9a6e1b152484d659c288cdaca409fbd.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，由安培力的取值范围可知电流的取值范围为<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/0262eeff73b945299e1c22069bc2111b.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> A≤<i>I</i>≤4 A</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设电流为<i>I</i><sub>1</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/83751682d2ca472db25612872ae15e13/30a3439e674d4bd78223b4269aa2ab49.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>
    A时滑动变阻器接入电路中的阻值为<i>R</i><sub>1</sub>，由闭合电路欧姆定律，有<i>E</i>－<i>I</i><sub>1</sub><i>r</i>＝<i>I</i><sub>1</sub>(<i>R</i><sub>0</sub>＋<i>R</i><sub>1</sub>)，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    代入数据可得<i>R</i><sub>1</sub>＝30 Ω</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设电流为<i>I</i><sub>2</sub>＝4
    A时滑动变阻器接入电路中的阻值为<i>R</i><sub>2</sub>，由闭合电路欧姆定律，有<i>E</i>－<i>I</i><sub>2</sub><i>r</i>＝<i>I</i><sub>2</sub>(<i>R</i><sub>0</sub>＋<i>R</i><sub>2</sub>)，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    代入数据可得<i>R</i><sub>2</sub>＝0</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    所以滑动变阻器接入电路中的阻值范围为0≤<i>R</i>≤30 Ω.</p>
</p><br>

<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业8 磁场2</h1>

<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">60 V</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">粒子运动轨迹如图所示：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/f6f937f9d6674557bd77070d108a4f14.png?"
        style="width:147px;height:130px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>根据洛伦兹力公式<i>F</i>＝<i>qvB</i>可知，磁感应强度一定时，粒子进入磁场的速度越大，在磁场中偏转量越小．故当磁感应强度取最大值时，若粒子恰好不飞离屏，则加速电压有最小值．设此时粒子刚好打在屏的最下端<i>B</i>点，根据带电粒子在磁场中运动特点可知，粒子偏离方向的夹角正切值为tan
    <i>θ</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/dd4bfb59321e47168afff2562dad9131.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，解得：tan <i>θ</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/a65daec18c0a4262a731a3557be207ee.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，粒子偏离方向的夹角：<i>θ</i>＝60°＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/2b25780211dc45cab98e78f19f5d9b4f.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由几何关系可知，此时粒子在磁场中对应的回旋半径为：<i>R</i>＝<i>r</i>tan<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/b371ad85e2774984915ad91b74a0cd0d.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝0．1<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/a65daec18c0a4262a731a3557be207ee.png?"
        style="height:22px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> m&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;①</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    带电粒子在电场中加速，由动能定理得：<i>qU</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/92cb0382959340bfbf9249d89f202881.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><i>mv</i><sup>2</sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;②</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">带电粒子在磁场中偏转时，洛伦兹力提供向心力，
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由牛顿第二定律可得：<i>qvB</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/8ac00bc8f6de4af9942c585d56d7d0d1.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;③
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    联立①②③解得：<i>U</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/11ee8dec83b7491ba538899a53d05e25.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝60 V，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">故加速电压的最小值为60 V．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(1)0．1 T (2)30°</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)设粒子的初速度大小为<i>v</i>，粒子在极板间做匀速直线运动，则有：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>qvB</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>qE</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    设粒子在圆形区域中做匀速圆周运动的半径为<i>r</i>，则有：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>qvB</i><sub>2</sub>＝<i>m</i><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/e74b2fb33b20405eb356a29c365964a7.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">粒子速度方向偏转了60°，有</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>r</i>＝2<i>R</i>sin 60°
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    解得：<i>B</i><sub>2</sub>＝0．1 T．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)撤去磁场<i>B</i><sub>1</sub>后，粒子在极板间做类平抛运动，设在板间运动时间为<i>t</i>，运动的加速度为<i>a</i>，飞出电场时竖直方向的速度为<i>v</i><sub>y</sub>，则有：
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>qE</i>＝<i>ma</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><i>l</i>＝<i>vt</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>v</i><sub>y</sub>＝<i>at</i></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">tan
    <i>θ</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/74cf41baae1d43b7b3132ed738751713.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解得：tan
    <i>θ</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/0b6437d6a24242a8b8e09d3f7a659ac3.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，即<i>θ</i>＝30°．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(1)<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/44baa1f8909e4b888b5ac0cf6e051820.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/0347cb0d0f3f435c987ef5dabc09a689.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><i>L</i>＋<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/949e4be39a6d4d68a792c50f8b23dc6d.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> (2)<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/7b67185b5f23447c91c84b246b05b360.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/4c84c24658f14f638d4bbf9bfa0d219d.png?"
        style="width:129px;height:112px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)粒子<i>a</i>竖直向下穿过<i>OC</i>，在磁场中轨迹圆心如图甲为<i>O</i><sub>1</sub>，<i>OO</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>R</i>cot
    <i>θ</i>，<i>OO</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>L</i>－<i>R</i> </p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">得粒子圆周运动的轨迹半径</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>R</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/720571f5cb2e45509d2c5ad44eeda46a/0347cb0d0f3f435c987ef5dabc09a689.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><i>L</i>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;①</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由洛伦兹力提供圆周运动向心力有：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>qv</i><sub>1</sub><i>B</i>＝<span>​</span><img

<h1>2021级高二物理寒假作业9 电磁感应1</h1>
<h2>多选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>A</p><br>
<p><strong>05.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>06.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>07.</strong>A,C</p><br>
<p><strong>08.</strong>B,D</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)向下 (2)BCD</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)金属弦靠近螺线管时，线圈中磁场变强，根据楞次定律可得通过放大器的电流方向为向下．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)感应电动势的大小与磁通量的变化率有关，与线圈匝数有关，所以选项B、C正确；电吉他通过扩音器发出的声音频率与感应电流的频率相同，即与金属弦振动频率相同，A错误，D正确．</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)0.4 V (2)0.16 W (3)2
    s</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)由法拉第电磁感应定律得</p>

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<i>n</i>×<span>​</span><img

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/f93212320e5b479d9dbc3a871cb6e33b.png?"

    W.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(3)分析线圈受力可知，当细线松弛时有：</p>

    s.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> (1)3.2×10<sup>－2</sup> N
    (2)1.28×10<sup>－2</sup> J</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (1)无论磁场方向是竖直向上还是竖直向下，当两金属细杆都以速度<i>v</i>朝相反方向滑动时，两金属细杆产生大小相同方向一致的感应电动势．</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>E</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>E</i><sub>2</sub>＝<i>Bdv</i>①</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由闭合电路欧姆定律，回路中的电流</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>I</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/9df94132dddb43a195fa328bd147df2c.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>②</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    因拉力与安培力平衡，作用于每根金属杆的拉力大小为<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>＝<i>BdI</i>③</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    由①②③联立并代入数据，得<i>F</i><sub>1</sub>＝<i>F</i><sub>2</sub>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/5556ca79435e46fba0d20cbfdec88630.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/918366ca0b304c43899a9759e3dd9a9e.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span> N＝3.2×10<sup>－2</sup> N.</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (2)设金属杆之间增加的距离为Δ<i>L</i>，则两金属杆共产生的热量<i>Q</i>＝<i>I</i><sup>2</sup>·2<i>r</i>·<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/48cc6182877c4d82ad35a2b2831e833a.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>，</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    代入数据得<i>Q</i>＝1.28×10<sup>－2</sup> J.</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"> 2<i>mg</i>sin <i>θ</i>
    <span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/fb24b6746e56459682361868a0977e35.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    当<i>ab</i>杆沿导轨上滑达到最大速度<i>v</i>时，其受力如图所示：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">由平衡条件可知：</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    <i>F</i>－<i>F</i><sub>B</sub>＝<i>mg</i>sin
    <i>θ</i>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;①
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    又<i>F</i><sub>B</sub>＝<i>BIL</i>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;②
</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/04303a8f677a40a39ce977b608a53693.png?"
        style="width:123px;height:96px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>而<i>I</i>＝<span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/b2f37aa899f64069b289307d36e5bff2/77f447e1166d4fb7aa787861d01dd9d9.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;③

        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span>＝0</p>

    联立④⑤两式解得：<i>F</i>＝2<i>mg</i>sin <i>θ</i></p>

    <i>v</i>＝<span>​</span><img

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/4ce5ffe26fee40f3b19375d32f431830/85c56ca2d74a4baf9c7dfbcd4c9481b4.png?"

        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/16/4ce5ffe26fee40f3b19375d32f431830/1d772d4320e842e59b9a7372ac0cf62b.png?"
        style="height:44px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span></p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    代入数据解得<i>Q</i><sub>1</sub>＝3 J.</p>

    (3)<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/380b4c30dc2047fa82f2564c209af0d9/10c0403f8c3140a7b52255f66674ff08.png?"
        style="width:48px;height:121px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/380b4c30dc2047fa82f2564c209af0d9/367db68165c74a1fb85e847e6d682c14.png?"
        style="width:75px;height:121px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/380b4c30dc2047fa82f2564c209af0d9/d18180e50abd41f1bb1f9586a67e42e8.png?"
        style="width:115px;height:121px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>、<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/380b4c30dc2047fa82f2564c209af0d9/2ab9e6eff7354bbeaa99aeca6c008346.png?"
        style="width:114px;height:91px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span> (写出两种即可)</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">(4)保护酚羟基，防止被高锰酸钾氧化 (5)8 2
    (6)9</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif"><span
        style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">解析</span>
    (1)甲苯中苯环以及与苯环相连的碳原子共12个原子一定共面，单键可以旋转，所以经旋转甲基上有一个氢原子可以与苯环共面，最多有13个原子共面。</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (4)后续步骤中需要将苯环上的甲基氧化成羧基，酚羟基易被氧化，所以反应⑤的目的是保护酚羟基，防止被高锰酸钾氧化。</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','KaiTi','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (5)产物A与足量氢气加成得到的产物为<span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/380b4c30dc2047fa82f2564c209af0d9/44d1d733d57a4a5987831fe6d6cdb856.png?"
        style="width:84px;height:94px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span>，环上有6种环境的氢原子，取代基上有2种环境的氢原子，所以核磁共振氢谱有8组峰；1 mol产物B含有1 mol普通酯基，可以消耗1 mol
    NaOH，含有1 mol酚羟基可以消耗1 mol NaOH，共可以与2 mol NaOH反应。</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    (6)采取“定二移一”的分析方法，先固定—COOCH<sub>3</sub>和—OH，二者处于邻位，则—COCH<sub>3</sub>有4种位置；二者处于间位，则—COCH<sub>3</sub>有4种位置；二者处于对位，则—COCH<sub>3</sub>有2种位置，所以包括B在内共有10种结构，则产物B的同分异构体(不包括B)有9种。
</p>
</p><br>

    mol F与足量的饱和NaHCO<sub>3</sub>溶液反应可产生2
    mol二氧化碳，则F中含有2个羧基，因此E为二甲苯，E苯环上的一氯代物只有2种，E为<span>​</span><span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/c99f9c0c59c442cfb88460f740cef96a/0e68544b92194b2db57f6f25bcf5328c.png?"
        style="width:70px;height:45px;display:inline-block"
        alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span><span>​</span>，则F为<span>​</span><span>​</span><span>​</span><img
        src="http://ezy-word2html-imgs.oss-cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/2022-12/29/c99f9c0c59c442cfb88460f740cef96a/463d3ddc245f4084853369cccc34f8f6.png?"
        style="width:86px;height:45px;display:inline-block" alt=""><span>​</span><span>​</span><span>​</span>。</p>

<h1>2021级高二化学寒假作业7 生物大分子</h1>
<h2>单选题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>03.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>04.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>05.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>06.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>07.</strong>C</p><br>
<p><strong>08.</strong>D</p><br>
<p><strong>09.</strong>B</p><br>
<p><strong>10.</strong>D</p><br>
<hr>
<h2>解答题</h2>
<p><strong>01.</strong>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    没有加入氢氧化钠溶液调节pH，使溶液呈碱性，再加银氨溶液。</p>
<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','SimSun','Microsoft YaHei',Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">
    在蔗糖溶液中加入3~5滴稀硫酸；将混合液煮沸几分钟，冷却；在冷却后的溶液呈酸性，没有加入氢氧化钠溶液调节pH，使溶液呈碱性，导致加入的银氨溶液和酸反应，实验结果没有银镜产生。</p>
</p><br>
<p><strong>02.</strong>

<h1>2021级高二化学寒假作业8 化学反应中的热效应</h1>
